/* You may insert all settings here eg: SET LINESIZE 120*/

DROP TABLE Candidates_report; 
DROP TABLE Advertisement;                  
DROP TABLE Interview;      
DROP TABLE Job_candidates;       
DROP TABLE Job;
DROP TABLE Manager;
DROP TABLE Department;
DROP TABLE Company;                     
DROP TABLE Job_category;        
DROP TABLE Resume;             
          

CREATE TABLE Resume
(resume_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
job_history_desc VARCHAR(40),
job_start DATE,
job_end DATE,
min_salary NUMBER(8,2),
max_salary NUMBER(8,2),
PRIMARY KEY(resume_id));


CREATE TABLE Job_category
(job_category_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
job_category_type VARCHAR(40),
PRIMARY KEY(job_category_id));


CREATE TABLE Company
(company_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
company_location VARCHAR(50),
company_category VARCHAR(20),
company_desc VARCHAR(65),
company_name VARCHAR(50),
PRIMARY KEY(company_id));


CREATE TABLE Department 
(department_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
department_name VARCHAR(30), 
company_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
department_desc VARCHAR(30),
PRIMARY KEY(department_id),
FOREIGN KEY (company_id) REFERENCES Company(company_id ));


CREATE TABLE Manager
(manager_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
manager_name VARCHAR (30), 
department_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
manager_position VARCHAR(40),
PRIMARY KEY(manager_id),
FOREIGN KEY (department_id) REFERENCES Department(department_id));


CREATE TABLE Job
(job_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
job_name VARCHAR(40), 
job_desc VARCHAR(40), 
job_category_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
company_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
job_position VARCHAR(30),
PRIMARY KEY(job_id),
FOREIGN KEY (company_id) REFERENCES Company(company_id),
FOREIGN KEY (job_category_id) REFERENCES Job_category(job_category_id ));


CREATE TABLE Job_candidates
(candidate_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
resume_id VARCHAR(7), 
location VARCHAR(60), 
candidate_email VARCHAR(40), 
candidate_name VARCHAR(40),
PRIMARY KEY(candidate_id),
FOREIGN KEY (resume_id) REFERENCES Resume(resume_id));


CREATE TABLE Interview
(interview_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
candidate_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
accept VARCHAR(10),  
job_id VARCHAR(7), 
interview_date_time TIMESTAMP, 
interview_way VARCHAR(6), 
interview_location VARCHAR(60), 
manager_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
PRIMARY KEY(interview_id),
FOREIGN KEY (manager_id) REFERENCES Manager(manager_id),
FOREIGN KEY (candidate_id) REFERENCES  Job_candidates(candidate_id),
FOREIGN KEY (job_id) REFERENCES Job(job_id));


CREATE TABLE Advertisement
(ads_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
ads_type VARCHAR(30), 
candidate_type VARCHAR(30), 
candidate_id VARCHAR(7), 
company_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
PRIMARY KEY(ads_id),
FOREIGN KEY (candidate_id) REFERENCES Job_candidates(candidate_id),
FOREIGN KEY (company_id) REFERENCES Company(company_id));


CREATE TABLE Candidates_report
(cand_report_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
Job_type_req VARCHAR(40), 
resume_id VARCHAR(7) not null, 
department_id VARCHAR(7) not null,
PRIMARY KEY(cand_report_id),
FOREIGN KEY (resume_id) REFERENCES Resume(resume_id),
FOREIGN KEY (department_id) REFERENCES Department(department_id));

COMMIT;

SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfJobCandidates
FROM Job_candidates;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfAdvertisement
FROM Advertisement;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfResume
FROM Resume;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfInterview
FROM Interview;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfJob
FROM Job;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfJobCategory
FROM Job_category;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfCompany
FROM Company;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfDepartment
FROM Department;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfManager
FROM Manager;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS NoOfCandidatesReport
FROM Candidates_report;
